<script>

	function toggleDiv(id, val){
		  var div = document.getElementById(id);

		  if (div) {
		     div.style.display = val;
		  }
		}

function displayCourse(crn, semester, pe_term, myelement, frame_title, show_locations,subj_code, show_schedules ,w_crns) {
	  if ( (myelement < 999) && ($('#data_' + myelement).is(":visible"))) {
  		// hide course detail view
          $('#data_' + myelement).hide();
        // Remove the subject based class for the header
         $('#bgrnd_' + myelement).removeClass("slidetop " + subj_code);
        // show faculty name span
          $('#data_' + myelement).prev().find('span.professorname').show();
        // restyle course title & crn to list view
         // $('#data_' + myelement).prev().children('.coursecode_big').toggleClass('coursecode_big coursecode');
         $('#data_' + myelement).prev().children('.coursecode_big').addClass('coursecode');
         $('#data_' + myelement).prev().children('.coursecode_big').removeClass('coursecode_big');
   		 // $('#data_' + myelement).prev().children('.coursename_big').removeClass('col-xs-9');
   		 // $('#data_' + myelement).prev().children('.coursename_big').toggleClass('coursename_big coursename_small');
   		 $('#data_' + myelement).prev().children('.coursename_big').addClass('coursename_small');
   		 $('#data_' + myelement).prev().children('.coursename_big').removeClass('coursename_big');
	  }
	  else {
	  	// open detail view
	    $('#data_' + myelement).show();
        // Add the subject based class for the header
        $('#bgrnd_' + myelement).addClass("slidetop " + subj_code);

	    // hide faculty name span
	    $('#data_' + myelement).prev().find('span.professorname').hide();
	    // restyle course title & crn text for detail view
	    $('#data_' + myelement).prev().children('.coursecode').toggleClass('coursecode coursecode_big');
	    // $('#data_' + myelement).prev().children('.coursename_small').addClass('col-xs-9');
	    $('#data_' + myelement).prev().children('.coursename_small').toggleClass('coursename_small coursename_big');

	  var p_url= "display_single_course_cb.php";
	  var p_data = "crn=" + crn + "&semester=" + semester + "&pe_term=" +pe_term + "&frame_title=" + frame_title + "&show_locations=" + show_locations + "&show_schedules=" + show_schedules + "&w_crns=" + w_crns;
	  jQuery.ajax({
	  type: "POST",
	  url: p_url,
		data: {"crn":crn,"semester": semester, "pe_term":pe_term, "frame_title": frame_title, "show_locations": show_locations, "show_schedules":show_schedules, "w_crns":w_crns},
	   success: function(data) {
	 	  $('#data_'+myelement).html(data);
	 	  stButtons.locateElements();
		 }
	   });
	  }
	}

	function displayFeaturedCourse(crn, semester, pe_term, myelement, show_locations, show_schedules, w_crns) {

	  var p_url= "display_featured_course_cb.php";
	  // var p_data = "crn=" + crn + "&semester=" + semester + "&pe_term=" +pe_term + "&frame_title=" + frame_title + "&show_locations=" + show_locations;
	  var p_data = "crn=" + crn + "&semester=" + semester + "&pe_term=" +pe_term + "&show_locations=" + show_locations + "&show_schedules=" + show_schedules+ "&show_schedules=" + show_schedules + "&w_crns=" + w_crns;
	  jQuery.ajax({
	  type: "GET",
	  url: p_url,
	  data: p_data,
	   success: function(data) {
	 	  $('#data_'+myelement).html(data);
	 	  stButtons.locateElements();
		}
	  });
	}

	function setCookieAndToggle(v1, v2) {
	    var d = new Date();
	    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (5*60*1000)); // 5 minutes
	    var expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
	    document.cookie =  "hideCB=1; " + expires;
	    toggleDiv(v1,v2);
	    toggleDiv('show_featured','inline-block');
	    toggleDiv('hide_featured','none');
	}

	function clearCookieAndToggle(v1, v2) {
	    var d = new Date();
	    var expires = "expires=Thu, 01-Jan-1970 00:00:01 GMT;";
	    document.cookie =  "hideCB=0; " + expires;
	    toggleDiv(v1,v2);
	    toggleDiv('show_featured','none');
	    toggleDiv('hide_featured','inline-block');
	}


	function resetSubject(myform){
		// cycle through the options collection, setting the selected attribute of each to false
		subject.selected=false;
	}

	function resetDepartment(myform){
		//cycle through the options collection, setting the selected attribute of each to false
		department.selected=false;
	}


	function resetAll() {
		//document.forms[0].keywords.value = '';
		$("#keywords").val("");
		$("select").each(function() { this.selectedIndex = 0 });
		$(".distribution").select2("val", "");
		$('#waitlist_search_option').prop('checked', false);

	}

	 $(document).ready(function () {
	     $(".distribution").select2();
	   });
	

</script>
